You can also assign your own voice commands to an Action. \r\n\r\nSome of those Actions are: Select [word], Select from [word1] until [word2], Insert [word] before/after [some word], Delete [word], Capitalize [word], Round bracket [word], Select last sentence, and more. The voice commands referred to as Actions are explained in in-app video tutorials, and a printable user guide.\r\n\r\nIn fact, this description - as is - was voice typed using SpeechToText Pro and Actions.\r\n\r\nSpeechToText Pro will not do the following:\r\n\r\n1. Work without internet.\r\n\r\n2. Produce good results without a high-quality USB microphone. (For more details, see Resources -> Best Results.)\r\n\r\n3. Produce accurate results in the presence of background noise.\r\n\r\n4. Transcribe speeches delivered from a distant source, such as a public speaker.\r\n\r\n5. Convert audio files into text.\r\n\r\n6. Produce audio recordings. This is strictly a speech-to-text app! (Well, it does text-to-speech as well.)\r\n\r\nHere is what SpeechToText Pro will do:\r\n\r\n1) Convert spoken words into text at the rate of natural speech, and at near-100% accuracy.\r\n\r\n2) Allow you to modify existing text, or define the presentation of the text you are pronouncing, through the use of voice commands. Voice commands replace the mouse and keyboard. However, the option to modify text using those methods exists too.\r\n\r\n3) Let you substitute the predefined voice commands with your own.\r\n\r\n4) Offer support for hotkeys. Simply assign a voice command to a difficult-to-pronounce segment of text. Then pronounce the voice command for the difficult-to-pronounce text to print.\r\n\r\n5) Let you save text, send it as an email, send it as an SMS message, share it to other apps, upload it to OneDrive, play it back in a synthetic voice, or print it.\r\n\r\n6) Provide a convenient user interface for paraphrasing spoken content in Youtube videos.\r\n\r\n7) Let you do scientific calculator-level calculations with its voice-driven calculator.\r\n\r\n8) Help you protect your content by defining users. \r\n\r\n9) Allow you to produce richly formatted content that can be saved as an RTF file, PDF file, or printed. \r\n\r\nAlthough SpeechToText Pro has a learning curve, it is minimized thanks to its intuitive design, easy-to-read documentation, and the fact that every control (button, switch, menu) throughout the user interface is documented with a tooltip. Every major component of the app has its own user guide. The user guide on Actions can also be saved or printed. The information in the user guides is complemented by video tutorials, accessible through Resources -> Video Tutorials.\r\n\r\nIt is in the user's best interest to learn all the features of SpeechToText Pro so that this Windows 10 speech to text app can be used in its fullest potential.\r\n\r\nSpeechToText Pro has a free 24-hour trial period and then a price of $6.49.
